<h2 id="examples" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#examples"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Examples</h2>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8bhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8bhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8bhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="controlled" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#controlled"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Controlled</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">To create a controlled Pagination component, manage the state of the current page using the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">page</code> prop and update it
when the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">onPageChange</code> event handler is called:</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8hhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8hhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8hhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="root-provider" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#root-provider"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Root Provider</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">An alternative way to control the pagination is to use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">RootProvider</code> component and the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">usePagination</code> hook. This
way you can access the state and methods from outside the component.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8nhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8nhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8nhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="customization" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#customization"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Customization</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">You can customize the Pagination component by setting various props such as <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">dir</code>, <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">pageSize</code>, <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">siblingCount</code>, and
<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">translations</code>. Here&#x27;s an example of a customized Pagination:</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8thanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8thanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8thanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="context" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#context"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Context</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Access pagination state and methods with <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Pagination.Context</code> or the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">usePaginationContext</code> hook. You get methods like
<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">setPage</code>, <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">setPageSize</code>, <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">goToNextPage</code>, <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">goToPrevPage</code>, <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">goToFirstPage</code>, <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">goToLastPage</code>, as well as properties like
<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">totalPages</code> and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">pageRange</code>.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_93hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_93hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_93hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="data-slicing" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#data-slicing"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Data Slicing</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">slice()</code> method to paginate actual data arrays. This method automatically slices your data based on the current
page and page size.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_99hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_99hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_99hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="page-range" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#page-range"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Page Range</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Display the current page range information using the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">pageRange</code> property. This shows which items are currently visible
(e.g., &quot;Showing 1-10 of 100 results&quot;).</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_9fhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_9fhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_9fhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="page-size" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#page-size"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Page Size</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Control the number of items per page dynamically using <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">setPageSize()</code>. This example shows how to integrate a native
select element to change the page size.</p>
<blockquote class="mt_1.6em mb_1.6em ps_1em fw_500 font-style_italic bd-s-w_0.25rem bd-c_var(--colors-prose-quote-border)">
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Note:</strong> For uncontrolled behavior, use <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">defaultPageSize</code> to set the initial value. For controlled behavior, use
<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">pageSize</code> and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">onPageSizeChange</code> to programmatically manage the page size.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_9nhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_9nhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_9nhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="links" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#links"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Links</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Create pagination with link navigation for better SEO and accessibility. This example shows how to use the pagination
component with anchor links instead of buttons.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_9thanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_9thanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_9thanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h2 id="api-reference" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#api-reference"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>API Reference</h2>
<h3 id="props" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#props"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Props</h3>
<h3 class="text text--variant_heading text--size_xl">Root</h3><p class="text c_fg.muted">Renders a <code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">&lt;&gt;</code> element.</p><div class="bd-w_1px bdr_lg ov-x_auto my_8 not-prose"><table class="bd_0 table__root table__root--size_sm table__root--variant_outline"><thead class="table__head table__head--size_sm table__header--variant_outline">Prop</th><th class="px_4 bg_gray.2 h_10 table__header table__header--size_sm table__header--variant_outline">Default</th><th class="px_4 bg_gray.2 h_10 table__header table__header--size_sm table__header--variant_outline">Type</th></tr></thead><tbody class="table__body table__body--size_sm table__body--variant_outline"><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="w_36 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline c_colorPalette.default">asChild</code></td><td class="w_28 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" gap_1"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">boolean</code><p class="text">Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior.</p><span /\u003e\n\n## Anatomy\n\n\u003cAnatomy id=\"pagination\" /\u003e\n\n```tsx\n\u003cPagination.Root\u003e\n  \u003cPagination.PrevTrigger /\u003e\n  \u003cPagination.Item /\u003e\n  \u003cPagination.Ellipsis /\u003e\n  \u003cPagination.NextTrigger /\u003e\n\u003c/Pagination.Root\u003e\n```\n\n## Examples\n\n**Example: basic**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { ChevronLeftIcon, ChevronRightIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport { Pagination } from '@ark-ui/react/pagination'\nimport styles from 'styles/pagination.module.css'\n\nexport const Basic = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cPagination.Root count={5000} pageSize={10} siblingCount={2} className={styles.Root}\u003e\n    \u003cdiv className={styles.Controls}\u003e\n      \u003cPagination.PrevTrigger className={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n        \u003cChevronLeftIcon /\u003e\n      \u003c/Pagination.PrevTrigger\u003e\n      \u003cPagination.Context\u003e\n        {(pagination) =\u003e\n          pagination.pages.map((page, index) =\u003e\n            page.type === 'page' ? (\n              \u003cPagination.Item key={index} {...page} className={styles.Item}\u003e\n                {page.value}\n              \u003c/Pagination.Item\u003e\n            ) : (\n              \u003cPagination.Ellipsis key={index} index={index} className={styles.Ellipsis}\u003e\n                \u0026#8230;\n              \u003c/Pagination.Ellipsis\u003e\n            ),\n          )\n        }\n      \u003c/Pagination.Context\u003e\n      \u003cPagination.NextTrigger className={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n        \u003cChevronRightIcon /\u003e\n      \u003c/Pagination.NextTrigger\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  \u003c/Pagination.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { ChevronLeftIcon, ChevronRightIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { Pagination } from '@ark-ui/solid/pagination'\nimport { For } from 'solid-js'\nimport styles from 'styles/pagination.module.css'\n\nexport const Basic = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cPagination.Root count={5000} pageSize={10} siblingCount={2} class={styles.Root}\u003e\n    \u003cdiv class={styles.Controls}\u003e\n      \u003cPagination.PrevTrigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n        \u003cChevronLeftIcon /\u003e\n      \u003c/Pagination.PrevTrigger\u003e\n      \u003cPagination.Context\u003e\n        {(pagination) =\u003e (\n          \u003cFor each={pagination().pages}\u003e\n            {(page, index) =\u003e\n              page.type === 'page' ? (\n                \u003cPagination.Item {...page} class={styles.Item}\u003e\n                  {page.value}\n                \u003c/Pagination.Item\u003e\n              ) : (\n                \u003cPagination.Ellipsis index={index()} class={styles.Ellipsis}\u003e\n                  \u0026#8230;\n                \u003c/Pagination.Ellipsis\u003e\n              )\n            }\n          \u003c/For\u003e\n        )}\n      \u003c/Pagination.Context\u003e\n      \u003cPagination.NextTrigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n        \u003cChevronRightIcon /\u003e\n      \u003c/Pagination.NextTrigger\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  \u003c/Pagination.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { ChevronLeft, ChevronRight } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport { Pagination } from '@ark-ui/vue/pagination'\nimport styles from 'styles/pagination.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cPagination.Root :count=\"5000\" :page-size=\"10\" :sibling-count=\"2\" :class=\"styles.Root\"\u003e\n    \u003cdiv :class=\"styles.Controls\"\u003e\n      \u003cPagination.PrevTrigger :class=\"styles.Trigger\"\u003e\n        \u003cChevronLeft /\u003e\n      \u003c/Pagination.PrevTrigger\u003e\n      \u003cPagination.Context v-slot=\"pagination\"\u003e\n        \u003ctemplate v-for=\"(page, index) in pagination.pages\" :key=\"index\"\u003e\n          \u003cPagination.Item v-if=\"page.type === 'page'\" v-bind=\"page\" :class=\"styles.Item\"\u003e\n            {{ page.value }}\n          \u003c/Pagination.Item\u003e\n          \u003cPagination.Ellipsis v-else :index=\"index\" :class=\"styles.Ellipsis\"\u003e\u0026#8230;\u003c/Pagination.Ellipsis\u003e\n        \u003c/template\u003e\n      \u003c/Pagination.Context\u003e\n      \u003cPagination.NextTrigger :class=\"styles.Trigger\"\u003e\n        \u003cChevronRight /\u003e\n      \u003c/Pagination.NextTrigger\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  \u003c/Pagination.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { ChevronLeft, ChevronRight } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import { Pagination } from '@ark-ui/svelte/pagination'\n  import styles from 'styles/pagination.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cPagination.Root count={5000} pageSize={10} siblingCount={2} class={styles.Root}\u003e\n  \u003cdiv class={styles.Controls}\u003e\n    \u003cPagination.PrevTrigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n      \u003cChevronLeft /\u003e\n    \u003c/Pagination.PrevTrigger\u003e\n    \u003cPagination.Context\u003e\n      {#snippet render(pagination)}\n        {#each pagination().pages as page, index (index)}\n          {#if page.type === 'page'}\n            \u003cPagination.Item {...page} class={styles.Item}\u003e\n              {page.value}\n            \u003c/Pagination.Item\u003e\n          {:else}\n            \u003cPagination.Ellipsis {index} class={styles.Ellipsis}\u003e\u0026#8230;\u003c/Pagination.Ellipsis\u003e\n          {/if}\n        {/each}\n      {/snippet}\n    \u003c/Pagination.Context\u003e\n    \u003cPagination.NextTrigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n      \u003cChevronRight /\u003e\n    \u003c/Pagination.NextTrigger\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/Pagination.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Controlled\n\nTo create a controlled Pagination component, manage the state of the current page using the `page` prop and update it\nwhen the `onPageChange` event handler is called:\n\n**Example: controlled**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { ChevronLeftIcon, ChevronRightIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport { useState } from 'react'\nimport { Pagination } from '@ark-ui/react/pagination'\nimport styles from 'styles/pagination.module.css'\n\nexport const Controlled = () =\u003e {\n  const [currentPage, setCurrentPage] = useState(1)\n\n  return (\n    \u003cPagination.Root\n      count={5000}\n      pageSize={10}\n      siblingCount={2}\n      page={currentPage}\n      onPageChange={(details) =\u003e setCurrentPage(details.page)}\n      className={styles.Root}\n    \u003e\n      \u003cdiv className={styles.Controls}\u003e\n        \u003cPagination.PrevTrigger className={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n          \u003cChevronLeftIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Pagination.PrevTrigger\u003e\n        \u003cPagination.Context\u003e\n          {(pagination) =\u003e\n            pagination.pages.map((page, index) =\u003e\n              page.type === 'page' ? (\n                \u003cPagination.Item key={index} {...page} className={styles.Item}\u003e\n                  {page.value}\n                \u003c/Pagination.Item\u003e\n              ) : (\n                \u003cPagination.Ellipsis key={index} index={index} className={styles.Ellipsis}\u003e\n                  \u0026#8230;\n                \u003c/Pagination.Ellipsis\u003e\n              ),\n            )\n          }\n        \u003c/Pagination.Context\u003e\n        \u003cPagination.NextTrigger className={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n          \u003cChevronRightIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Pagination.NextTrigger\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n    \u003c/Pagination.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { ChevronLeftIcon, ChevronRightIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { Pagination } from '@ark-ui/solid/pagination'\nimport { For, createSignal } from 'solid-js'\nimport styles from 'styles/pagination.module.css'\n\nexport const Controlled = () =\u003e {\n  const [currentPage, setCurrentPage] = createSignal(1)\n\n  return (\n    \u003cPagination.Root\n      count={5000}\n      pageSize={10}\n      siblingCount={2}\n      page={currentPage()}\n      onPageChange={(details) =\u003e setCurrentPage(details.page)}\n      class={styles.Root}\n    \u003e\n      \u003cdiv class={styles.Controls}\u003e\n        \u003cPagination.PrevTrigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n          \u003cChevronLeftIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Pagination.PrevTrigger\u003e\n        \u003cPagination.Context\u003e\n          {(pagination) =\u003e (\n            \u003cFor each={pagination().pages}\u003e\n              {(page, index) =\u003e\n                page.type === 'page' ? (\n                  \u003cPagination.Item {...page} class={styles.Item}\u003e\n                    {page.value}\n                  \u003c/Pagination.Item\u003e\n                ) : (\n                  \u003cPagination.Ellipsis index={index()} class={styles.Ellipsis}\u003e\n                    \u0026#8230;\n                  \u003c/Pagination.Ellipsis\u003e\n                )\n              }\n            \u003c/For\u003e\n          )}\n        \u003c/Pagination.Context\u003e\n        \u003cPagination.NextTrigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n          \u003cChevronRightIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Pagination.NextTrigger\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n    \u003c/Pagination.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { ChevronLeft, ChevronRight } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport { Pagination } from '@ark-ui/vue/pagination'\nimport { ref } from 'vue'\nimport styles from 'styles/pagination.module.css'\n\nconst currentPage = ref(1)\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cPagination.Root :count=\"5000\" :page-size=\"10\" :sibling-count=\"2\" v-model:page=\"currentPage\" :class=\"styles.Root\"\u003e\n    \u003cdiv :class=\"styles.Controls\"\u003e\n      \u003cPagination.PrevTrigger :class=\"styles.Trigger\"\u003e\n        \u003cChevronLeft /\u003e\n      \u003c/Pagination.PrevTrigger\u003e\n      \u003cPagination.Context v-slot=\"pagination\"\u003e\n        \u003ctemplate v-for=\"(page, index) in pagination.pages\" :key=\"index\"\u003e\n          \u003cPagination.Item v-if=\"page.type === 'page'\" v-bind=\"page\" :class=\"styles.Item\"\u003e\n            {{ page.value }}\n          \u003c/Pagination.Item\u003e\n          \u003cPagination.Ellipsis v-else :index=\"index\" :class=\"styles.Ellipsis\"\u003e\u0026#8230;\u003c/Pagination.Ellipsis\u003e\n        \u003c/template\u003e\n      \u003c/Pagination.Context\u003e\n      \u003cPagination.NextTrigger :class=\"styles.Trigger\"\u003e\n        \u003cChevronRight /\u003e\n      \u003c/Pagination.NextTrigger\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  \u003c/Pagination.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { ChevronLeft, ChevronRight } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import { Pagination } from '@ark-ui/svelte/pagination'\n  import styles from 'styles/pagination.module.css'\n\n  let page = $state(1)\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cPagination.Root count={5000} pageSize={10} siblingCount={2} bind:page class={styles.Root}\u003e\n  \u003cdiv class={styles.Controls}\u003e\n    \u003cPagination.PrevTrigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n      \u003cChevronLeft /\u003e\n    \u003c/Pagination.PrevTrigger\u003e\n    \u003cPagination.Context\u003e\n      {#snippet render(pagination)}\n        {#each pagination().pages as page, index (index)}\n          {#if page.type === 'page'}\n            \u003cPagination.Item {...page} class={styles.Item}\u003e\n              {page.value}\n            \u003c/Pagination.Item\u003e\n          {:else}\n            \u003cPagination.Ellipsis {index} class={styles.Ellipsis}\u003e\u0026#8230;\u003c/Pagination.Ellipsis\u003e\n          {/if}\n        {/each}\n      {/snippet}\n    \u003c/Pagination.Context\u003e\n    \u003cPagination.NextTrigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n      \u003cChevronRight /\u003e\n    \u003c/Pagination.NextTrigger\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/Pagination.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Root Provider\n\nAn alternative way to control the pagination is to use the `RootProvider` component and the `usePagination` hook. This\nway you can access the state and methods from outside the component.\n\n**Example: root-provider**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { ChevronLeftIcon, ChevronRightIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport { Pagination, usePagination } from '@ark-ui/react/pagination'\nimport styles from 'styles/pagination.module.css'\n\nexport const RootProvider = () =\u003e {\n  const pagination = usePagination({ count: 5000, pageSize: 10, siblingCount: 2 })\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv className=\"stack\"\u003e\n      \u003cbutton className={styles.Trigger} onClick={() =\u003e pagination.goToNextPage()}\u003e\n        Next Page\n      \u003c/button\u003e\n\n      \u003cPagination.RootProvider value={pagination} className={styles.Root}\u003e\n        \u003cdiv className={styles.Controls}\u003e\n          \u003cPagination.PrevTrigger className={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n            \u003cChevronLeftIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/Pagination.PrevTrigger\u003e\n          \u003cPagination.Context\u003e\n            {(pagination) =\u003e\n              pagination.pages.map((page, index) =\u003e\n                page.type === 'page' ? (\n                  \u003cPagination.Item key={index} {...page} className={styles.Item}\u003e\n                    {page.value}\n                  \u003c/Pagination.Item\u003e\n                ) : (\n                  \u003cPagination.Ellipsis key={index} index={index} className={styles.Ellipsis}\u003e\n                    \u0026#8230;\n                  \u003c/Pagination.Ellipsis\u003e\n                ),\n              )\n            }\n          \u003c/Pagination.Context\u003e\n          \u003cPagination.NextTrigger className={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n            \u003cChevronRightIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/Pagination.NextTrigger\u003e\n        \u003c/div\u003e\n      \u003c/Pagination.RootProvider\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { ChevronLeftIcon, ChevronRightIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { Pagination, usePagination } from '@ark-ui/solid/pagination'\nimport { For } from 'solid-js'\nimport styles from 'styles/pagination.module.css'\n\nexport const RootProvider = () =\u003e {\n  const pagination = usePagination({ count: 5000, pageSize: 10, siblingCount: 2 })\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n      \u003cbutton class={styles.Trigger} onClick={() =\u003e pagination().goToNextPage()}\u003e\n        Next Page\n      \u003c/button\u003e\n\n      \u003cPagination.RootProvider value={pagination} class={styles.Root}\u003e\n        \u003cdiv class={styles.Controls}\u003e\n          \u003cPagination.PrevTrigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n            \u003cChevronLeftIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/Pagination.PrevTrigger\u003e\n          \u003cPagination.Context\u003e\n            {(pagination) =\u003e (\n              \u003cFor each={pagination().pages}\u003e\n                {(page, index) =\u003e\n                  page.type === 'page' ? (\n                    \u003cPagination.Item {...page} class={styles.Item}\u003e\n                      {page.value}\n                    \u003c/Pagination.Item\u003e\n                  ) : (\n                    \u003cPagination.Ellipsis index={index()} class={styles.Ellipsis}\u003e\n                      \u0026#8230;\n                    \u003c/Pagination.Ellipsis\u003e\n                  )\n                }\n              \u003c/For\u003e\n            )}\n          \u003c/Pagination.Context\u003e\n          \u003cPagination.NextTrigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n            \u003cChevronRightIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/Pagination.NextTrigger\u003e\n        \u003c/div\u003e\n      \u003c/Pagination.RootProvider\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { ChevronLeft, ChevronRight } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport { Pagination, usePagination } from '@ark-ui/vue/pagination'\nimport styles from 'styles/pagination.module.css'\n\nconst pagination = usePagination({ count: 5000, pageSize: 10, siblingCount: 2 })\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n    \u003cbutton :class=\"styles.Trigger\" @click=\"pagination.goToNextPage()\"\u003eNext Page\u003c/button\u003e\n\n    \u003cPagination.RootProvider :value=\"pagination\" :class=\"styles.Root\"\u003e\n      \u003cdiv :class=\"styles.Controls\"\u003e\n        \u003cPagination.PrevTrigger :class=\"styles.Trigger\"\u003e\n          \u003cChevronLeft /\u003e\n        \u003c/Pagination.PrevTrigger\u003e\n        \u003cPagination.Context v-slot=\"pagination\"\u003e\n          \u003ctemplate v-for=\"(page, index) in pagination.pages\" :key=\"index\"\u003e\n            \u003cPagination.Item v-if=\"page.type === 'page'\" v-bind=\"page\" :class=\"styles.Item\"\u003e\n              {{ page.value }}\n            \u003c/Pagination.Item\u003e\n            \u003cPagination.Ellipsis v-else :index=\"index\" :class=\"styles.Ellipsis\"\u003e\u0026#8230;\u003c/Pagination.Ellipsis\u003e\n          \u003c/template\u003e\n        \u003c/Pagination.Context\u003e\n        \u003cPagination.NextTrigger :class=\"styles.Trigger\"\u003e\n          \u003cChevronRight /\u003e\n        \u003c/Pagination.NextTrigger\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n    \u003c/Pagination.RootProvider\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { ChevronLeft, ChevronRight } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import { Pagination, usePagination } from '@ark-ui/svelte/pagination'\n  import styles from 'styles/pagination.module.css'\n\n  const id = $props.id()\n  const pagination = usePagination({\n    id,\n    count: 5000,\n    pageSize: 10,\n    siblingCount: 2,\n  })\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n  \u003cbutton class={styles.Trigger} onclick={() =\u003e pagination().goToNextPage()}\u003eNext Page\u003c/button\u003e\n\n  \u003cPagination.RootProvider value={pagination} class={styles.Root}\u003e\n    \u003cdiv class={styles.Controls}\u003e\n      \u003cPagination.PrevTrigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n        \u003cChevronLeft /\u003e\n      \u003c/Pagination.PrevTrigger\u003e\n\n      {#each pagination().pages as page, index (index)}\n        {#if page.type === 'page'}\n          \u003cPagination.Item {...page} class={styles.Item}\u003e\n            {page.value}\n          \u003c/Pagination.Item\u003e\n        {:else}\n          \u003cPagination.Ellipsis {index} class={styles.Ellipsis}\u003e\u0026#8230;\u003c/Pagination.Ellipsis\u003e\n        {/if}\n      {/each}\n\n      \u003cPagination.NextTrigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n        \u003cChevronRight /\u003e\n      \u003c/Pagination.NextTrigger\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  \u003c/Pagination.RootProvider\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Customization\n\nYou can customize the Pagination component by setting various props such as `dir`, `pageSize`, `siblingCount`, and\n`translations`. Here's an example of a customized Pagination:\n\n**Example: customized**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { ChevronLeftIcon, ChevronRightIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport { Pagination } from '@ark-ui/react/pagination'\nimport styles from 'styles/pagination.module.css'\n\nexport const Customized = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cPagination.Root\n    count={5000}\n    pageSize={20}\n    siblingCount={3}\n    translations={{\n      nextTriggerLabel: 'Next',\n      prevTriggerLabel: 'Prev',\n      itemLabel: (details) =\u003e `Page ${details.page}`,\n    }}\n    className={styles.Root}\n  \u003e\n    \u003cdiv className={styles.Controls}\u003e\n      \u003cPagination.PrevTrigger className={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n        \u003cChevronLeftIcon /\u003e\n      \u003c/Pagination.PrevTrigger\u003e\n      \u003cPagination.Context\u003e\n        {(pagination) =\u003e\n          pagination.pages.map((page, index) =\u003e\n            page.type === 'page' ? (\n              \u003cPagination.Item key={index} {...page} className={styles.Item}\u003e\n                {page.value}\n              \u003c/Pagination.Item\u003e\n            ) : (\n              \u003cPagination.Ellipsis key={index} index={index} className={styles.Ellipsis}\u003e\n                \u0026#8230;\n              \u003c/Pagination.Ellipsis\u003e\n            ),\n          )\n        }\n      \u003c/Pagination.Context\u003e\n      \u003cPagination.NextTrigger className={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n        \u003cChevronRightIcon /\u003e\n      \u003c/Pagination.NextTrigger\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  \u003c/Pagination.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { ChevronLeftIcon, ChevronRightIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { Pagination } from '@ark-ui/solid/pagination'\nimport { For } from 'solid-js'\nimport styles from 'styles/pagination.module.css'\n\nexport const Customized = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cPagination.Root\n      count={5000}\n      pageSize={20}\n      siblingCount={3}\n      translations={{\n        nextTriggerLabel: 'Next',\n        prevTriggerLabel: 'Prev',\n        itemLabel: (details) =\u003e `Page ${details.page}`,\n      }}\n      class={styles.Root}\n    \u003e\n      \u003cdiv class={styles.Controls}\u003e\n        \u003cPagination.PrevTrigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n          \u003cChevronLeftIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Pagination.PrevTrigger\u003e\n        \u003cPagination.Context\u003e\n          {(pagination) =\u003e (\n            \u003cFor each={pagination().pages}\u003e\n              {(page, index) =\u003e\n                page.type === 'page' ? (\n                  \u003cPagination.Item {...page} class={styles.Item}\u003e\n                    {page.value}\n                  \u003c/Pagination.Item\u003e\n                ) : (\n                  \u003cPagination.Ellipsis index={index()} class={styles.Ellipsis}\u003e\n                    \u0026#8230;\n                  \u003c/Pagination.Ellipsis\u003e\n                )\n              }\n            \u003c/For\u003e\n          )}\n        \u003c/Pagination.Context\u003e\n        \u003cPagination.NextTrigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n          \u003cChevronRightIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Pagination.NextTrigger\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n    \u003c/Pagination.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { ChevronLeft, ChevronRight } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport { Pagination } from '@ark-ui/vue/pagination'\nimport styles from 'styles/pagination.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cPagination.Root\n    :count=\"5000\"\n    :page-size=\"20\"\n    :sibling-count=\"3\"\n    :translations=\"{\n      nextTriggerLabel: 'Next',\n      prevTriggerLabel: 'Prev',\n      itemLabel: (details) =\u003e `Page ${details.page}`,\n    }\"\n    :class=\"styles.Root\"\n  \u003e\n    \u003cdiv :class=\"styles.Controls\"\u003e\n      \u003cPagination.PrevTrigger :class=\"styles.Trigger\"\u003e\n        \u003cChevronLeft /\u003e\n      \u003c/Pagination.PrevTrigger\u003e\n      \u003cPagination.Context v-slot=\"pagination\"\u003e\n        \u003ctemplate v-for=\"(page, index) in pagination.pages\" :key=\"index\"\u003e\n          \u003cPagination.Item v-if=\"page.type === 'page'\" v-bind=\"page\" :class=\"styles.Item\"\u003e\n            {{ page.value }}\n          \u003c/Pagination.Item\u003e\n          \u003cPagination.Ellipsis v-else :index=\"index\" :class=\"styles.Ellipsis\"\u003e\u0026#8230;\u003c/Pagination.Ellipsis\u003e\n        \u003c/template\u003e\n      \u003c/Pagination.Context\u003e\n      \u003cPagination.NextTrigger :class=\"styles.Trigger\"\u003e\n        \u003cChevronRight /\u003e\n      \u003c/Pagination.NextTrigger\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  \u003c/Pagination.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { ChevronLeft, ChevronRight } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import { Pagination } from '@ark-ui/svelte/pagination'\n  import styles from 'styles/pagination.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cPagination.Root\n  count={5000}\n  pageSize={20}\n  siblingCount={3}\n  translations={{\n    nextTriggerLabel: 'Next',\n    prevTriggerLabel: 'Prev',\n    itemLabel: (details) =\u003e `Page ${details.page}`,\n  }}\n  class={styles.Root}\n\u003e\n  \u003cdiv class={styles.Controls}\u003e\n    \u003cPagination.PrevTrigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n      \u003cChevronLeft /\u003e\n    \u003c/Pagination.PrevTrigger\u003e\n    \u003cPagination.Context\u003e\n      {#snippet render(pagination)}\n        {#each pagination().pages as page, index (index)}\n          {#if page.type === 'page'}\n            \u003cPagination.Item {...page} class={styles.Item}\u003e\n              {page.value}\n            \u003c/Pagination.Item\u003e\n          {:else}\n            \u003cPagination.Ellipsis {index} class={styles.Ellipsis}\u003e\u0026#8230;\u003c/Pagination.Ellipsis\u003e\n          {/if}\n        {/each}\n      {/snippet}\n    \u003c/Pagination.Context\u003e\n    \u003cPagination.NextTrigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n      \u003cChevronRight /\u003e\n    \u003c/Pagination.NextTrigger\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/Pagination.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Context\n\nAccess pagination state and methods with `Pagination.Context` or the `usePaginationContext` hook. You get methods like\n`setPage`, `setPageSize`, `goToNextPage`, `goToPrevPage`, `goToFirstPage`, `goToLastPage`, as well as properties like\n`totalPages` and `pageRange`.\n\n**Example: context**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { ChevronLeftIcon, ChevronRightIcon, ChevronsLeftIcon, ChevronsRightIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport { Pagination } from '@ark-ui/react/pagination'\nimport styles from 'styles/pagination.module.css'\n\nexport const Context = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cPagination.Root count={100} pageSize={10} className={styles.Root}\u003e\n      \u003cPagination.Context\u003e\n        {(pagination) =\u003e (\n          \u003cdiv className={styles.Controls}\u003e\n            \u003cbutton className={styles.Trigger} onClick={() =\u003e pagination.goToFirstPage()}\u003e\n              \u003cChevronsLeftIcon /\u003e\n            \u003c/button\u003e\n            \u003cbutton className={styles.Trigger} onClick={() =\u003e pagination.goToPrevPage()}\u003e\n              \u003cChevronLeftIcon /\u003e\n            \u003c/button\u003e\n            \u003cp className={styles.Text} style={{ minWidth: '120px', textAlign: 'center' }}\u003e\n              Page {pagination.page} of {pagination.totalPages}\n            \u003c/p\u003e\n            \u003cbutton className={styles.Trigger} onClick={() =\u003e pagination.goToNextPage()}\u003e\n              \u003cChevronRightIcon /\u003e\n            \u003c/button\u003e\n            \u003cbutton className={styles.Trigger} onClick={() =\u003e pagination.goToLastPage()}\u003e\n              \u003cChevronsRightIcon /\u003e\n            \u003c/button\u003e\n          \u003c/div\u003e\n        )}\n      \u003c/Pagination.Context\u003e\n    \u003c/Pagination.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { ChevronLeftIcon, ChevronRightIcon, ChevronsLeftIcon, ChevronsRightIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { Pagination } from '@ark-ui/solid/pagination'\nimport styles from 'styles/pagination.module.css'\n\nexport const Context = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cPagination.Root count={100} pageSize={10} class={styles.Root}\u003e\n      \u003cPagination.Context\u003e\n        {(pagination) =\u003e (\n          \u003cdiv class={styles.Controls}\u003e\n            \u003cbutton class={styles.Trigger} onClick={() =\u003e pagination().goToFirstPage()}\u003e\n              \u003cChevronsLeftIcon /\u003e\n            \u003c/button\u003e\n            \u003cbutton class={styles.Trigger} onClick={() =\u003e pagination().goToPrevPage()}\u003e\n              \u003cChevronLeftIcon /\u003e\n            \u003c/button\u003e\n            \u003cp class={styles.Text} style={{ 'min-width': '120px', 'text-align': 'center' }}\u003e\n              Page {pagination().page} of {pagination().totalPages}\n            \u003c/p\u003e\n            \u003cbutton class={styles.Trigger} onClick={() =\u003e pagination().goToNextPage()}\u003e\n              \u003cChevronRightIcon /\u003e\n            \u003c/button\u003e\n            \u003cbutton class={styles.Trigger} onClick={() =\u003e pagination().goToLastPage()}\u003e\n              \u003cChevronsRightIcon /\u003e\n            \u003c/button\u003e\n          \u003c/div\u003e\n        )}\n      \u003c/Pagination.Context\u003e\n    \u003c/Pagination.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { ChevronLeft, ChevronRight, ChevronsLeft, ChevronsRight } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport { Pagination } from '@ark-ui/vue/pagination'\nimport styles from 'styles/pagination.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cPagination.Root :count=\"100\" :page-size=\"10\" :class=\"styles.Root\"\u003e\n    \u003cPagination.Context v-slot=\"pagination\"\u003e\n      \u003cdiv :class=\"styles.Controls\"\u003e\n        \u003cbutton :class=\"styles.Trigger\" @click=\"pagination.goToFirstPage()\"\u003e\n          \u003cChevronsLeft /\u003e\n        \u003c/button\u003e\n        \u003cbutton :class=\"styles.Trigger\" @click=\"pagination.goToPrevPage()\"\u003e\n          \u003cChevronLeft /\u003e\n        \u003c/button\u003e\n        \u003cp :class=\"styles.Text\" style=\"min-width: 120px; text-align: center\"\u003e\n          Page {{ pagination.page }} of {{ pagination.totalPages }}\n        \u003c/p\u003e\n        \u003cbutton :class=\"styles.Trigger\" @click=\"pagination.goToNextPage()\"\u003e\n          \u003cChevronRight /\u003e\n        \u003c/button\u003e\n        \u003cbutton :class=\"styles.Trigger\" @click=\"pagination.goToLastPage()\"\u003e\n          \u003cChevronsRight /\u003e\n        \u003c/button\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n    \u003c/Pagination.Context\u003e\n  \u003c/Pagination.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { ChevronLeft, ChevronRight, ChevronsLeft, ChevronsRight } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import { Pagination } from '@ark-ui/svelte/pagination'\n  import styles from 'styles/pagination.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cPagination.Root count={100} pageSize={10} class={styles.Root}\u003e\n  \u003cPagination.Context\u003e\n    {#snippet render(pagination)}\n      \u003cdiv class={styles.Controls}\u003e\n        \u003cbutton class={styles.Trigger} onclick={() =\u003e pagination().goToFirstPage()}\u003e\n          \u003cChevronsLeft /\u003e\n        \u003c/button\u003e\n        \u003cbutton class={styles.Trigger} onclick={() =\u003e pagination().goToPrevPage()}\u003e\n          \u003cChevronLeft /\u003e\n        \u003c/button\u003e\n        \u003cp class={styles.Text} style=\"min-width: 120px; text-align: center;\"\u003e\n          Page {pagination().page} of {pagination().totalPages}\n        \u003c/p\u003e\n        \u003cbutton class={styles.Trigger} onclick={() =\u003e pagination().goToNextPage()}\u003e\n          \u003cChevronRight /\u003e\n        \u003c/button\u003e\n        \u003cbutton class={styles.Trigger} onclick={() =\u003e pagination().goToLastPage()}\u003e\n          \u003cChevronsRight /\u003e\n        \u003c/button\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n    {/snippet}\n  \u003c/Pagination.Context\u003e\n\u003c/Pagination.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Data Slicing\n\nUse the `slice()` method to paginate actual data arrays. This method automatically slices your data based on the current\npage and page size.\n\n**Example: data-slicing**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { ChevronLeftIcon, ChevronRightIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport { Pagination } from '@ark-ui/react/pagination'\nimport styles from 'styles/pagination.module.css'\n\nconst users = [\n  { id: 1, name: 'Emma Wilson', email: 'emma@example.com' },\n  { id: 2, name: 'Liam Johnson', email: 'liam@example.com' },\n  { id: 3, name: 'Olivia Brown', email: 'olivia@example.com' },\n  { id: 4, name: 'Noah Davis', email: 'noah@example.com' },\n  { id: 5, name: 'Ava Martinez', email: 'ava@example.com' },\n  { id: 6, name: 'Ethan Garcia', email: 'ethan@example.com' },\n  { id: 7, name: 'Sophia Rodriguez', email: 'sophia@example.com' },\n  { id: 8, name: 'Mason Lee', email: 'mason@example.com' },\n  { id: 9, name: 'Isabella Walker', email: 'isabella@example.com' },\n  { id: 10, name: 'James Hall', email: 'james@example.com' },\n  { id: 11, name: 'Mia Allen', email: 'mia@example.com' },\n  { id: 12, name: 'Benjamin Young', email: 'benjamin@example.com' },\n  { id: 13, name: 'Charlotte King', email: 'charlotte@example.com' },\n  { id: 14, name: 'William Wright', email: 'william@example.com' },\n  { id: 15, name: 'Amelia Scott', email: 'amelia@example.com' },\n  { id: 16, name: 'Henry Green', email: 'henry@example.com' },\n  { id: 17, name: 'Harper Adams', email: 'harper@example.com' },\n  { id: 18, name: 'Sebastian Baker', email: 'sebastian@example.com' },\n  { id: 19, name: 'Evelyn Nelson', email: 'evelyn@example.com' },\n  { id: 20, name: 'Jack Carter', email: 'jack@example.com' },\n]\n\nexport const DataSlicing = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cPagination.Root count={users.length} pageSize={5} className={styles.Root}\u003e\n      \u003cPagination.Context\u003e\n        {(pagination) =\u003e (\n          \u003c\u003e\n            \u003cdiv className={styles.Grid}\u003e\n              {pagination.slice(users).map((user) =\u003e (\n                \u003cdiv key={user.id} className={styles.GridItem}\u003e\n                  \u003cspan className={styles.GridItemTitle}\u003e{user.name}\u003c/span\u003e\n                  \u003cspan className={styles.GridItemText}\u003e{user.email}\u003c/span\u003e\n                \u003c/div\u003e\n              ))}\n            \u003c/div\u003e\n\n            \u003cdiv className={styles.Controls}\u003e\n              \u003cPagination.PrevTrigger className={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n                \u003cChevronLeftIcon /\u003e\n              \u003c/Pagination.PrevTrigger\u003e\n\n              {pagination.pages.map((page, index) =\u003e\n                page.type === 'page' ? (\n                  \u003cPagination.Item key={index} {...page} className={styles.Item}\u003e\n                    {page.value}\n                  \u003c/Pagination.Item\u003e\n                ) : (\n                  \u003cPagination.Ellipsis key={index} index={index} className={styles.Ellipsis}\u003e\n                    \u0026#8230;\n                  \u003c/Pagination.Ellipsis\u003e\n                ),\n              )}\n\n              \u003cPagination.NextTrigger className={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n                \u003cChevronRightIcon /\u003e\n              \u003c/Pagination.NextTrigger\u003e\n            \u003c/div\u003e\n          \u003c/\u003e\n        )}\n      \u003c/Pagination.Context\u003e\n    \u003c/Pagination.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Range\n\nDisplay the current page range information using the `pageRange` property. This shows which items are currently visible\n(e.g., \"Showing 1-10 of 100 results\").\n\n**Example: page-range**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { ChevronLeftIcon, ChevronRightIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport { Pagination } from '@ark-ui/react/pagination'\nimport styles from 'styles/pagination.module.css'\n\nexport const PageRange = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cPagination.Root count={100} pageSize={10} className={styles.Root}\u003e\n      \u003cPagination.Context\u003e\n        {(pagination) =\u003e (\n          \u003c\u003e\n            \u003cdiv className={styles.Controls}\u003e\n              \u003cPagination.PrevTrigger className={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n                \u003cChevronLeftIcon /\u003e\n              \u003c/Pagination.PrevTrigger\u003e\n\n              {pagination.pages.map((page, index) =\u003e\n                page.type === 'page' ? (\n                  \u003cPagination.Item key={index} {...page} className={styles.Item}\u003e\n                    {page.value}\n                  \u003c/Pagination.Item\u003e\n                ) : (\n                  \u003cPagination.Ellipsis key={index} index={index} className={styles.Ellipsis}\u003e\n                    \u0026#8230;\n                  \u003c/Pagination.Ellipsis\u003e\n                ),\n              )}\n\n              \u003cPagination.NextTrigger className={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n                \u003cChevronRightIcon /\u003e\n              \u003c/Pagination.NextTrigger\u003e\n            \u003c/div\u003e\n\n            \u003cdiv className=\"stack\"\u003e\n              \u003cp className={styles.Text}\u003e\n                Showing {pagination.pageRange.start + 1}-{pagination.pageRange.end} of {pagination.count} results\n              \u003c/p\u003e\n              \u003cp className={styles.Text}\u003e\n                Page {pagination.page} of {pagination.totalPages}\n              \u003c/p\u003e\n            \u003c/div\u003e\n          \u003c/\u003e\n        )}\n      \u003c/Pagination.Context\u003e\n    \u003c/Pagination.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { ChevronLeftIcon, ChevronRightIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { Pagination } from '@ark-ui/solid/pagination'\nimport {             \u003cPagination.Ellipsis index={index()} class={styles.Ellipsis}\u003e\n                      \u0026#8230;\n                    \u003c/Pagination.Ellipsis\u003e\n                  )\n                }\n              \u003c/For\u003e\n\n              \u003cPagination.NextTrigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n                \u003cChevronRightIcon /\u003e\n              \u003c/Pagination.NextTrigger\u003e\n            \u003c/div\u003e\n\n            \u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n              \u003cp class={styles.Text}\u003e\n                Showing {pagination().pageRange.start + 1}-{pagination().pageRange.end} of {pagination().count} results\n              \u003c/p\u003e\n              \u003cp class={styles.Text}\u003e\n                Page {pagination().page} of {pagination().totalPages}\n              \u003c/p\u003e\n            \u003c/div\u003e\n          \u003c/\u003e\n        )}\n      \u003c/Pagination.Context\u003e\n    \u003c/Pagination.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { ChevronLeft, ChevronRight } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport { Pagination } from '@ark-ui/vue/pagination'\nimport styles from 'styles/pagination.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cPagination.Root :count=\"100\" :page-size=\"10\" \u003c/p\u003e\n        \u003cp :class=\"styles.Text\"\u003ePage {{ pagination.page }} of {{ pagination.totalPages }}\u003c/p\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n    \u003c/Pagination.Context\u003e\n \u003cPagination.Context\u003e\n    {#snippet render(pagination)}\n      \u003cdiv class={styles.Controls}\u003e\n        \u003cPagination.PrevTrigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n
